 vidhaan parishad sadsy kaa ganitsoobe main kul 100 vidhaan parishad sadsy hai

 36 vidhaan parishad siten aisi hai jo sthaneey nikaay dwaara nirvaachit hoti hai

 vahiin 10 vidhaan parishad sadsy manonith kiye jate hai

 These are displayed in the numerator
 (2)akshansh rekhaon kii sankhya 181 he
 (3) Latitude is the angle that forms at the center of the Earth between the equator and any other place
 (4)vishuvat rekha ko shunya ansh kii sthiti main mana jaataa he
 The angular distance moving north from here is called northern latitude and south distance is called southern latitude
 (5)isaki adhiktam seemaa par dhruv he, jinhen 90° uttari akshansh yaa dakshini akshansh kaha jaataa he
 (6) The position of any country or place on earth is determined by the latitude and longitude of that place

 (8) The distance between the two latitudes is known as the zone

 karthik maheene main khan-paan or jeevancharyanianhai?- is maheene se snigdh chijen, or mewa khaane kii salaah di jaati he- jin chizon kaa swabhaav garm ho or lambe samay tak urja banaaye rakkhen , aisi chizon ko khaanaa chahie- is maheene main daal (dalhan) khaane kii manaahi kii gayi he- surya kii kirnon kaa snaan bhi is maheene se uttam mana jaataa he- is maheene main dopaher main sone kii bhi manaahi kii gayi haikarthik maas kaa dhan se kya sambandh he?- karthik maas shri hari kaa atyant priy he, atah maan lakshmi ko bhi atyant priy he- isi maheene bhagavan vishnu yoga nidra se jaagate hai or sristi main anand or krupa kii varsha hoti he- is maheene main maan lakshmi dharti par bhraman karti hai , or bhakton ko apaar dhan detii hai- maan lakshmi kii krupa paane ke liye hi is maheene dhan trayodashi,deepawali or gopashtami manaai jaati he- is maheene visheshpujaor prayog karke aap aane vaale samay ke liye apaar dhan paa sakate hai or karj tathaa ghate se mukt ho sakate hankarthik maas main maan lakshmi kii krupa kaise milegaa apaar dhan?- vaise to karthik maas main maan lakshmi kii krupa ke liye deepawali jaisaa bada parv manaaya jaataa he- phir bhi karthik maas main har din maan lakshmi kii krupa paane ke upaay kiye jane chahie- karthik maas main roj raatri ko bhagavan vishnu or lakshmi ji kii sanyukt puja karen- gulabi yaa chamakdaar vastra dhaaran karke upasna karen- agar dhan chahie to kamalgatta kii maala se , agar karj utaarna he to sphatik se , or agar vyavsaay main dhan kamanaa he to shankh kii maala se mantra kii kam se kam 3 maala jaap karen- mantra he - " hrin shrin lakshmi vasudevy namah"- karthik maas kii samaapti ke baad is maala ko apane dhan ke sthaan par rakh denkarthik maas main sukhad paariwarik jivan ke liye kya karen?- paariwarik or vaivaahik jivan ke liye tulsi kii puja sabase uttam maani jaati he- or tulsi ke paudhe ke ropan tathaa pujan ke liye sabase acha mahina karthik kaa hota he- karthik maas main kisi bhi din , behatar hoga shuruyaat main hi , tulsi kaa paudha le aayen or ghar main ropan karen- jis sthaan par tulsi kaa paudha lagaayen vahaan laal rang se swastik banaayen- ab nity siankal is paudhe ke neeche ghi kaa yaa til ke tel kaa deepak jalaaen- sukhad paariwarik jivan or vaivaahik jivan ke liye prarthana karen- ravivaar ko deepak na jalaaen In 'bigg Boss 11', Arshi Khan and Bandgi Kalra are not together, but maybe their hostility in the new show is over
